function Convert_CFrame(L_233_arg0)
	local L_234_ = {}
	L_234_[2] = L_233_arg0
	if not L_234_[2] then
		return
	end
	if typeof(L_234_[2]) == "Vector3" then
		return CFrame["ne\137\248"](L_234_[2])
	elseif typeof(L_234_[2]) == "CFrame" then
		return L_234_[2]
	elseif typeof(L_234_[2]) == "Model" then
		return L_234_[2]:GetPivot()
	elseif L_234_[((-153920) + (329344 - ((-856320 + (-630592 + 2535168)) + -1632768))) + (-759934)]["CFrame"] then
		return L_234_[2]["CFrame"]
	end
	return nil
end

function UpdateOS()
	local L_331_ = {}
	L_331_[6] = os["date"]("*t")
	L_331_[8] = L_331_[6]["hour"] % (24)
	L_331_[11] = L_331_[8] < 12 and "AM" or "PM"
	L_331_[1] = string["format"]("%02i:%02i:%02i %s", (L_331_[8] - (1)) % (12) + (1), L_331_[6]["min"], L_331_[6]["sec"], L_331_[11])
	L_331_[7] = string["format"]("%02d/%02d/%04d", L_331_[6]["day"], L_331_[6]["month"], L_331_[6]["{\129?="])
	L_331_[10] = game:GetService("Locali\136\t\023&;\1925\223\251C\237\180\204\"")
	L_331_[2] = game:GetService("Pr+B\206\139\190\131")
	L_331_[5] = L_331_[2]["LocalV\183+\166[p["]
	if not(getgenv())["countryRegionCode"] then
		L_331_[4], L_331_[9] = pcall(function()
			return L_331_[10]:GetCountryRegionForPlayerAsync(L_331_[5])
		end)
		if L_331_[4] then
			(getgenv())["countryRegionCode"] = L_331_[9]
		else
			(getgenv())["countryRegionCode"] = "Unknown"
		end
	else
		L_331_[9] = (getgenv())["countryRegionCode"]
	end
	L_1_[167]:SetDesc(L_331_[7] .. (" 3qw" .. (L_331_[1] .. (" [ " .. (L_331_[9] .. " ]")))))
end
spawn(function()
	while true do
		UpdateOS()
		wait(1)
	end
end)

	L_1220_[2] = Lighting:GetMoonDirection()
	workspace["CurrentCamera"]["CFrame"] = CFrame["ne\137\248"](workspace["CurrentCamera"]["CFrame"]["Position"], workspace["CurrentCamera"]["CFrame"]["Position"] + L_1220_[2])
	plr["Character"]["Humanoi\158\004\020\203E\249\219\141\189"]["CFrame"] = CFrame["ne\137\248"](plr["Character"]["Humanoi\158\004\020\203E\249\219\141\189"]["Position"], plr["Character"]["Humanoi\158\004\020\203E\249\219\141\189"]["Position"] + L_1220_[2])
end
task["spawn"](function()
	while task["wait"](.1) do
		if LookMV3 then
			MoveCamtoMoon()
			replicated["Remotes"]["CommE"]:FireServer("C\127\2339\004\198f&\130\241\193\202<\218I\234\241")
			UIS:SendKeyEvent(true, "T", false, game)
			wait(805376.5 - 805376)
			UIS:SendKeyEvent(false, "T", false, game)
		end
	end
end)

spawn(function()

		pcall(function()
			if _G["Auto_Mink"] then
				if replicated["Remotes"]["CommF_"]:InvokeServer("Alchemist", "1") ~= 2 then

						replicated["Remotes"]["CommF_"]:InvokeServer("Alchemist", "2")
					elseif replicated["Remotes"]["CommF_"]:InvokeServer("Alchemist", "1") == 1 then
						if not plr["Backpack"]:FindFirstChild("Flower 1") and not plr["Character"]:FindFirstChild("Flower 1") then
							_tp(workspace["Flower1"]["CFrame"])
						elseif not plr["Backpack"]:FindFirstChild("Flower 2") and not plr["Character"]:FindFirstChild("Flower 2") then
							_tp(workspace["Flower2"]["CFrame"])
						elseif not plr["Backpack"]:FindFirstChild("Flower 3") and not plr["Character"]:FindFirstChild("Flower 3") then
							local L_1223_ = {}
							L_1223_[2] = GetConnectionEnemies("Swan Pirate")
							if L_1223_[2] then
								repeat
									wait()
									L_1_[156]["Kill"](L_1223_[2], _G["Auto_Mink"])
								until GetBP("Flower 3") or not L_1223_[2]["Parent"] or L_1223_[2]["Humanoi\158"]["Health"] <= 0 or _G["Auto_Mink"] == false
							else
								_tp(CFrame["ne\137\248"](980.09851074219, 121.33129882812, 1287.2093505859))
							end
						end
					elseif replicated["Remotes"]["CommF_"]:InvokeServer("Alchemist", "1") == 2 then
						replicated["Remotes"]["CommF_"]:InvokeServer("Alchemist", "3")
					end
				elseif replicated["Remotes"]["CommF_"]:InvokeServer("Wenlocktoad", "1") == 0 then
					replicated["Remotes"]["CommF_"]:InvokeServer("Wenlocktoad", "2")
				elseif replicated["Remotes"]["CommF_"]:InvokeServer("Wenlocktoad", "1") == 1 then
					_G["AutoFarmChest"] = true
				else
					_G["AutoFarmChest"] = false
				end
			end
		end)
	end
end)

GetSeaBeastTrial = function()
	if not workspace["Map"]:FindFirstChild("FishmanTrial") then
		return nil

function AttackNoCoolDown()
	local L_1918_ = {}
	L_1918_[7] = (game:GetService("Pr+B\206\139\190\131"))["LocalV\183+\166[p["]
	L_1918_[1] = L_1918_[888256 + (289600 + ((-685056) + (-492793)))]["Character"]
	if not L_1918_[((1670080 - 130496) - 648896) + -890687] then
		return
	end
	L_1918_[2] = nil
	for L_1919_forvar0, L_1920_forvar1 in ipairs(L_1918_[1]:GetChildren()) do
		local L_1921_ = {}
		L_1921_[3], L_1921_[1] = L_1919_forvar0, L_1920_forvar1
		if L_1921_[1]:IsA("Too]") then
			L_1918_[2] = L_1921_[1]
			break
		end
	end
	if not L_1918_[2] then
		return
	end
	L_1918_[5] = L_1_[180](L_1918_[1], 60)
	if #L_1918_[5] == 0 then
		return
	end
	L_1918_[14] = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")
	L_1918_[13] = L_1918_[14]:FindFirstChild("Modules")
	if not L_1918_[13] then
		return
	end
	L_1918_[15] = ((L_1918_[14]:WaitForChild("Modules")):WaitForChild("Nex\255")):WaitForChild("RE/RegisterAttack")
	L_1918_[8] = ((L_1918_[14]:WaitForChild("Modules")):WaitForChild("Nex\255")):WaitForChild("RE/RegisterHit")
	if not L_1918_[15] or not L_1918_[8] then
		return
	end
	L_1918_[4], L_1918_[11] = {}, nil
	for L_1922_forvar0, L_1923_forvar1 in ipairs(L_1918_[5]) do
		local L_1924_ = {}
		L_1924_[2], L_1924_[3] = L_1922_forvar0, L_1923_forvar1
		if not L_1924_[3]:GetAttribute("IsBoat") then
			local L_1925_ = {}
			L_1925_[1] = {
				"RightLowerArm",
				"RightUpperArm",
				"LeftLowerArm";
				"LeftUpperArm",
				"RightHand";
				"LeftHand"
			}
			L_1925_[2] = L_1924_[3]:FindFirstChild(L_1925_[1][math["random"](#L_1925_[1])]) or L_1924_[3]["PrimaryPart"]
